CALL FOR PAPERS

We invite members of the LatinIberianAmerican Association of
  Operations Research ALIO and the worldwide Operational
  Research OR community to take part in the
  XVII LatinIberianAmerican Conference on Operations Research
  held jointly with the III Conference of the Mexican Society of
  Operations Research CLAIOCSMIO  in Monterrey Mexico
  October   The academic program will consist of parallel
  technical plenary talks tutorials and short courses
  covering several aspects of OR


ABSTRACT  PAPER SUBMISSION

To participate an abstract of  characters must be submitted Additionally 
an page paper going through a review process may be submitted

Papers and abstracts may be written in Spanish English or
  Portuguese the three official languages of CLAIO  Accepted papers
  of registered authors will be published in the conference proceedings
  CDROM with an ISBN  All accepted abstracts will be published in
  the conference book of abstracts

A postconference special issue of "Annals of Operations Research"
  devoted to the best works of the conference will be published
  See details in the conference web site


IMPORTANT DATES

Mar	Optional Paper submission deadline extended deadline
May	Abstract submission deadline
May	Paper acceptancerejection notification
Jun	Abstract acceptancerejection notification
Jun	Cameraready paper deadline
Jul     Early registration deadline

 El Departamento de ComputaciFn del CINVESTAVIPN Unidad
 Zacatenco en MExico DF tiene una plaza de investigador
 de tiempo completo disponible para ocuparse inmediatamente

 El candidato a ocupar esta plazas debe tener un
 doctorado en ciencias de la computaciFn o un Erea afEDn
 y un perfil sFlido de investigaciFn o un buen potencial
 para desarrollar dicho perfil Todas las Ereas de computaciFn
 son bienvenidas aunque se darE preferencia a las Ereas
 existentes en el departamento La plaza puede ocuparla
 tanto un investigador joven reciEn doctorado como uno
 consolidado Nivel  o  en el SNI En ambos casos se
 considerarE de vital importancia que el candidato pueda
 cumplir con los estEndares para pertenecer al Sistema
 Nacional de Investigadores Se hace notar que la categorEDa y
 el salario otorgados estarEn en funciFn de la productividad
 cientEDfica y formaciFn de recursos humanos del candidato aunque
 en general los salarios del CINVESTAVIPN son altamente
 competitivos a nivel nacional

 El CINVESTAVIPN es el centro pFAblico de investigaciFn mEs
 importante de MExico con  investigadores de tiempo completo
 y una de las productividades cientEDficas mEs elevadas del
 paEDs El CINVESTAVIPN no cuenta con estudios de licenciatura
 sino sFlo de posgrado maestrEDa y doctorado por lo que la
 carga docente es muy ligera ya que se busca que la actividad
 preponderante sea la investigaciFn tanto bEsica como
 aplicada

 El Programa de Posgrado en ComputaciFn del CINVESTAVIPN

 de maestrEDa y doctorado Tanto el programa de maestrEDa como
 el de doctorado se encuentran en el PadrFn Nacional de Posgrado
 de CONACyT como "consolidados" con lo cual nuestros estudiantes
 reciben becas completas para cursar sus estudios Los proyectos de
 investigaciFn actuales del Departamento de ComputaciFn abarcan
 entre otras las Ereas de optimizaciFn sistemas de tiempo real
 trabajo cooperativo cFmputo reconfigurable paralelismo hardware
 reconfigurable criptografEDa computaciFn evolutiva visualizaciFn
 y bases de datos

BODY Call for Collaboration Proposals FuturICT Latin America

The Latin American Node of FuturICT httpfuturictunammx  is launching
 a call to identify potential collaborators in Latin America with research 
groups within the FuturICT FET Flagship project httpfuturicteu 

FuturICT is a major project which aims at tackling the global challenges of
 humanity in the st century  Its goals structure and proposed methods 
can be found at httpwwwfuturicteutheprojectproposal

Latin American researchers companies organizations and governments inter
ested in participating in FuturICT are invited to submit a two page proposa
l describing their interests expertise and contact details The proposal 
should specify in which aspect of FuturICT the collaboration is proposed A
t the Latin American Node we will integrate the proposals and facilitate t
he contact with particular groups in Europe and elsewhere

Please submit your proposal before January th  to futurict@futurictu
nammx

                              EVOLVE 
        EVOLVE  A Bridge Between Probability Set Oriented Numerics
                  and Evolutionary Computation

               August   Mexico City Mexico

                       httpevolvecinvestavmx
 DDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDD

DDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDD

 Scope of the EVOLVE
 DDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDD
 The massive use and large applicability spectrum of evolutionary
 algorithms for reallife applications determined the need of
 establishing solid theoretical grounds Only to offer a few examples
 one may consider mathematical objects th at are sometimes difficult ando
r
 costly to calculate At the same time acknowledged new results show that
 evolutionary computation can provide in some cases good and fast
 estimators of these quantities Similarly the handling of large
 quantities of data may require the use of distributed environments where 
the
 probability of failure and the stability of the algorithms may need to be
 addressed What is more common practice confirms in many cases that theo
ry
 based results have the advantage of ensuring performance guarantee factor
s
 for evolutionary algorithms in areas as diverse as optimization
 bioinformatics
 or robotics

 The aim of the EVOLVE is to build a bridge between probability statistic
s
 set oriented numerics and evolutionary computing as to identify new
 common and challenging research aspects The conference is also intended
 to foster a growing interest for robust and efficient methods with a soun
d
 theoretical background EVOLVE is intended to unify theoryinspired metho
ds
 and cuttingedge techniques ensuring performance guarantee factors
 By gathering researchers with different backgrounds ranging from compute
r
 science to mathematics statistics and physics to name just a few a uni
fied
 view and vocabulary can emerge where the theoretical advancements may ech
o in
 different domains

 Summarizing the EVOLVE focuses on challenging aspects arising at the
 passage from theory to new paradigms and aims to provide a unified view w
hile
 raising questions related to reliability performance guarantees and
 modeling

 Topics
   Theoretical foundations of evolutionary type algorithms
   Models in biology branching processes dynamic population models
   Stochastic algorithms simulated annealing particle models and Marko
v
    chain Monte Carlo methods adaptive Monte Carlo quantum Monte Carlo
    methods MCMC methods particle methods
  Risk analysis rare events simulation sensitivity measures
  Applications bayesian statistics large networks analysis models in
   fluid mechanics financial mathematics molecular chemistry bacteriolo
gy
   epidemiology
  Set oriented numerics
  Stochastic optimization
    landscape analysis
    selftuning and selfadaptive techniques
    single multi and manyobjective optimization
    large scale highly multimodal or highdimensional problems
    bioinspired models  evolutionary programming swarm intelligence

 Invited Speakers
 DDDDDDDDDDDDDDDD

 Vo BaNgu University of Melbourne Australia
 Pedro LarraFaga Technical University of Madrid Spain
 Tony Lelievre Ecole des Ponts ParisTech France
 Eric Moulines Institut TElEcom  TElEcom ParisTech ENST Paris
 France
 JianQiao Sun University of California Merced USA

 Conference Chairs

 Pierrick Legrand University of Bordeaux  France

 Publication
 DDDDDDDDDDD

 The EVOLVE  will accept both fulllength papers and extended abstract
s
 to be presented at the conference Full length papers will be published
 in the Advances in Intelligend and Soft Computing book series of Springer

 Extended abstracts will be published on CDROM provided with ISSN and
 ISBN
 The postproceedings will include extended versions of the best
 papersabstracts presented at the EVOLVE  and will appear in the
 Studies in Computational Intelligence book series of Springer

 Imortand Dates
 DDDDDDDDDDDDDD

 March    Submission of fulllength manuscripts
 April    Notification of authors full length manuscripts
 May      Camera ready papers due
 May      Submission of abstracts
 May      Notification of authors abstracts
 August   Conference dates

 Conference Location
 DDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDD

 The EVOLVE  will be hosted by the Computer Science Department of the
 CINVESTAVIPN which is located in the campus Zacatenco in Mexico City
 Mexico

 AMPLN track de NLP en IBERAMIA 
BODY Estimados colegas de la AMPLN

Les escribo para avisarles de la realizaciFn de un track en temas afines

al procesamiento de lenguaje natural en la conferencia IBERAMIA  a
realizarse en Cartagena de Indias Colombia del  al  de noviembre
de  El llamado a trabajos general lo pueden consultar en
httpiberamiadsicupvescallforpapers

En particular los temas considerados para el track de NLP son los
siguientes

 Language Resources
 Morphology Syntax Semantics
 Lexicon and ontology development
 Information retrieval and question answering
 Information extraction
 Sentiment analysis and opinion mining
 Detection of irony sarcasm satire and metaphors
 Multilinguism and multimodality
 Domain and genre adaptation of datadriven NLP systems
 Statistical and Machine Learning Methods for natural language
 Text Mining and Natural Language Processing Applications
 Robust NLP for social media
 Authorship attribution and plagiarism detection

Las fechas importantes son

on in general and in particular in local search techniques

lutionary strategies to solve large scale multiobjective optimization prob
lems Hereby it is desired that he or she addresses both theoretical and p

Asunto AMPLN CFP SEPLN  Workshop on Iberian CrossLanguage NLP tasks
De     "Manuel Montes" <mmontesg@cccinaoepmx
Fecha  Jue  de Abril de   am
Para   todos@amplnorg


Apologies if you receive multiple copies of this message

Please distribute to colleagues


Call for Papers
ICL Workshop on Iberian CrossLanguage NLP tasks
September   Huelva Spain
in conjunction with the th Conference of the Spanish Society for
Natural Language Processing  SEPLN 


In the Iberian Peninsula five official languages coexist Basque
Catalan Galician Portuguese and Spanish Fostering multilinguality
and establishing strong links among the linguistic resources developed
for each language of the region is essential

Additionally a lack of published resources in some of these languages
exists Such lack propitiates a strong interrelation between them and
higher resourced languages such as English and Spanish

In order to favour the intrarelation among the peninsular languages
as well as the interrelation between them and foreign languages
different purpose multilingual NLP tools need to be developed

TOPICS OF INTEREST

Crosslanguage  multilingual

 text categorisation
 information retrieval
 question answering
 patent retrieval
 word sense disambiguation
 opinion mining
 lexical substitution
 text summarization
 text reuse analysis
 plagiarism detection
 paraphrasing for MT
 text similarity estimation
 similarity of Wikipedia across languages

These tasks are often based on statistical linguistic and
hybrid approaches Machine translation cognates exploitation
or semantic relatedness are examples of the multiple resources
available for the development of such tools

The workshop addresses researchers from different fields of natural
language processingcomputational linguistics text mining machine
learning pattern recognition information retrieval and machine
translation


IMPORTANT DATES

June          Submission of paper LNCS format  pages maximum
July          Notification of acceptance
July         Camera ready due
September     Workshop day

SUBMISSIONS

Please submit your contribution to the ICL' workshop via EasyChair
httpswwweasychairorgconferences?conficl Each submission
will be blind reviewed by at least two members of the Program Committee
The papers will be published as CEUR Workshop Proceedings


ORGANISING COMMITTEE

th International Symposium on Ubiquitous Computing and Ambient
Intelligence UCAmI 
Riviera Maya Mexico December  
httpmamiuclmesucami

Selected papers will be published in the following journals

       Science of Computer Programming JCR Indexed
       Interacting with computers JCR indexed
       Sensors JCR indexed
       Journal of Ambient Intelligence & Humanized Computing not  JCR
indexed

Keynote speaker confirmed  Anind K Dey Carnegie Mellon University
HCI Institute Pittsburgh PA

Important dates
Paper submission June  
Notification of acceptance July  
Cameraready version September  
Conference dates December  

Conference background & goals

The Ubiquitous Computing UC idea envisioned by Weiser in  has
recently evolved to a more general paradigm known as Ambient Intelligence
AmI Ambient Intelligence then represents a new generation of
usercentred computing environments aiming to find new ways to obtain a
better integration of the information technology in everyday life devices
and activities

AmI environments are integrated by several autonomous computational
devices of modern life ranging from consumer electronics to mobile phones
Ideally people in an AmI environment will not notice these devices but
they will benefit from the services they provide them Such devices are
aware of the people present in those environments by reacting to their
gestures actions and context Recently the interest in Ambient
Intelligence Environments has grown considerably due to new challenges
posed by society giving place to new interesting associated research
disciplines such as vehicular ad hoc networks VANET Ambient Assisted
Living AAL eHealth Internet of Things and Home Automation among
others



Topics of interest

Human Interaction in Ambient Intelligence
          HumanCentric Interfaces for AmI environments multimodal
touchcomputing NFC D codes
          Context and Locationaware Frameworks and Sensing context
modelling useradaptability automatic generation of user interfaces
sentient computing  knowledgebased approaches affective and social
interfaces etc
          Virtual reality augmented reality smart objectsmediated and
tangible interactions applied to AmI
          Ubiquitous and ambient displays environments wall displays
urban displays multiscreen environments
          Detection and support for collaboration user intentions and
activity recognition analysis of psychological user states

ICT instrumentation of Smart Environments and Objects
          Mobile Ad Hoc Networks and wireless sensor networks WSNs
          RFID and D codes for realworld labelling
          Wearable Computing

Software Engineering aspects of Ubiquitous Computing and Ambient Intelligence
          New computing paradigms for AmI agents affective computing
autonomic computing cloud computing
          Cross cutting middleware concerns in AmI aspectoriented
programming for service discovery security data delivery
coordination
          Addressing nonfunctional facets of AmI realtime quality of
service fault tolerance
          Semantic middleware infrastructure Semantic Web OSGi DLNA
DPWS Triple Spaces Digital TV home automation standards PP
          Design patterns programming languages and environments for
better AmI programming and deployment
          Modeldriven architectures software verification and testing
frameworks and tools for AmI

Adding intelligence for Environment Adaptation
          Knowledge representation and management for user and
environment modelling and understanding Ontologies Semantic Web
Logic Expert Systems Multiagents
          Autonomic computing responsive and proactive systems and
dynamic reconfiguration
          Ontologies for user and environment modelling and understanding
          Learning reasoning and adaptation techniques over context models
          Collaborative Smart objects

Key application domains for Ambient Intelligence
          Ambient Assisted Living
          Internet of Things and Social Web of Things
          Social robotics
          Vehicular ad hoc networks VANETs and Intelligent Transport
Systems ITS
          Home Automation standards



Submission format and procedure
Long papers  pages and short papers  pages can be submitted  A
Doctoral Consortium will be created where PhD students are invited to
present the topic and progress of their research in order to obtain
feedback from a panel of experts The length of these papers should be no
longer than  pages Finally we expect no more than five satellite
workshops
 Submissions httpmamiuclmesucamiindexphpcontributions

       Jesús Favela CICESE México

  RANDOMNESS THROUGH COMPUTATION Some Answers More Questions
  Edited by H Zenil member of this mail discussion group
  World Scientific Publishing Company
  httpwwwworldscibookscomcompscihtml

 your
 library and colleagues
 
  Description
  
 
  The review volume dedicated to the memory of Ray Solomonoff 
 consists
 of an indispensable set of chapters written by leading scholars
 scientists
 and researchers in the field of Randomness including related subfields
 specially but not limited to the strong developed connections to the
 Computability and Recursion Theory Highly respected indeed renowned
 in
 their areas of specialization many of these contributors are the
 founders
 of their fields The scope of "Randomness Through Computation" is
 novel
 Each contributor shares his personal views and anecdotes on the various
 reasons and motivations which led him to the study of the  They
 share their visions from their vantage and distinctive viewpoints In
 summary this is an opportunity to learn about the topic and its
 various
 angles from the leading thinkers

	??b?ZGVZWNjafNu? de plagios
BODY Estimados comnpaFeros

mi nombre es Paolo Rosso y soy un profesor de la Universidad 
Politecnica de Valencia EspaFa en estos dias de visita al IPN para 
impartir a los estudiantes de maestria y doctorado de los Drs Grigori 
Sidorov y Alexander Gelbukh justamente un tutorial sobre deteccion de 
plagio

Si estan interesados a probar el software libre de deteccion de 
plagio pueden descargarse desade mi pagina web en Research  
Supervision la tesis de maestria de Enrique Valles hay un capitulo 
dedicado a eso

Al mismo tiempo le informo que los sistemas de software libre no son 
lo mejor que hay con respecto a la deteccion de plagio y hay sistemas 
que han participado a la competencia internacional de deteccion de 
plagio que organizo con otros compaFeros httppanwebisde cuya 
prestaciones son mejores pero como primera aproximacion al problema 
que tienen el uso de software libre les podria valer

Si en el futuro no quedasen satisfechos con las prestaciones de los 
sistemas de software libre y necesitaran ayuda para que algunos de los 
estudiantes de que superviso y que estan haciendo su doctorado en la 
deteccion del plagio les desarrolles un sistema de deteccion de 
plagio no duden en contactarme

Saludos cordiales

Dr Paolo Rosso
Natural Language Engineering Lab
Dpto Sistemas InformEticos y ComputaciFn
Universidad PolitEcnica Valencia
Spain

email prosso at dsicupves

  Software herramientas tEcnicas para detecciFn de plagios

 Estimado Luis

 Como parte de nuestro proyecto de desarrollo de la plataforma
 tecnolFgica del Sistema de Universidad Virtual de la
 Universidad de Guadalajara estamos considerando seriamente la
 inclusiFn de mecanismos automatizados de detecciFn de plagios
 entre los estudiantes de nuestros programas educativos a
 distancia Aunque sabemos que existen aplicaciones
 comerciales con esta funcionalidad me parece que nuestro
 carEcter de universidad pFAblica incluyendo nuestra situaciFn
 econFmica nos obliga a contemplar la posibilidad de un
 proyecto de integraciFn y desarrollo de software libre para
 atender nuestra necesidad En este sentido quisiera poder
 consultar a la comunidad de REMIDEC sobre la existencia de
 software o herramientas no comerciales para atender el
 problema del plagio de tareas tEcnicas computacionales que
 pudieran ser particularmente FAtiles en este contexto y
 expertos interesados en el problema

 BFEs posible reenviar este mensaje a la lista o incluirlo en
 el boletEDn?

 Saludos
 Rafael

BODY Estimado Luis

Como parte de nuestro proyecto de desarrollo de la plataforma 
tecnológica del Sistema de Universidad Virtual de la Universidad de 
Guadalajara estamos considerando seriamente la inclusión de mecanismos 
automatizados de detección de plagios entre los estudiantes de nuestros 
programas educativos a distancia Aunque sabemos que existen 
aplicaciones comerciales con esta funcionalidad me parece que nuestro 
carácter de universidad pública incluyendo nuestra situación económica 
nos obliga a contemplar la posibilidad de un proyecto de integración y 
desarrollo de software libre para atender nuestra necesidad En este 
sentido quisiera poder consultar a la comunidad de REMIDEC sobre la 
existencia de software o herramientas no comerciales para atender el 
problema del plagio de tareas técnicas computacionales que pudieran ser 
particularmente útiles en este contexto y expertos interesados en el 
problema

¿Es posible reenviar este mensaje a la lista o incluirlo en el boletín?

Saludos
Rafael

From "CLOSER Secretariat" <CLOSER_Secretariat@mailvrespcom
Date  November   PM GMT

 LAST CFP CLOSER   Int'l Conf on Cloud Computing and Services Science
ReplyTo "CLOSER Secretariat" <replyfefcdecfae@uctsvrespcom


We would like to invite you to submit a paper to the st International
Conference on Cloud Computing CLOSER  
wwwclosersciteventsorg
Next year this conference will be held in Noordwijkerhout the
Netherlands during  of May and is sponsored by INSTICC in
cooperation with the Workflow Management Coalition WfMC ACM SIGMIS
EuroCloud and IICREST

The deadline for regular paper SUBMISSION is scheduled for November
th  
We look forward to receiving your paper submission with innovative
contributions in any of the following main topic areas
 Cloud Computing Fundamentals
 Services Science Foundation for Cloud Computing
 Cloud Computing Platforms and Applications
 Cloud Computing Enabling Technology


The conference program features a number of Keynote Lectures to be
delivered by distinguished worldclass researchers Their names are
now available at the conference Website
wwwclosersciteventsorgkeynote_speakersasp

Submitted papers will be  to a doubleblind review process All
accepted papers will be published in the conference proceedings under
an ISBN reference on paper and on CDROM support The proceedings
will be submitted for indexation by several major international
indexers including Thomson Reuters Conference Proceedings Citation
Index INSPEC DBLP and EI CPPI
Best paper awards will be distributed during the conference closing
session
All papers presented at the conference venue will be available at the
SciTePress Science and Technology Publications Digital Library
wwwscitepressorgDigitalLibrary

Please check further details at the CLOSER  conference website
wwwclosersciteventsorg There you will find detailed information
about the conference structure and its main topic areas This
conference is colocated with WEBIST  th International
Conference on Web Information Systems and Technologies 
wwwwebistorg and with CSEDU  rd International Conference on
Computer Supported Education  wwwcseduorg Registration to CLOSER
will enable free attendance to any sessions of all colocated events

Workshops and special sessions are also invited If you wish to
propose a workshop or a special session for example based on the
results of a specific research project please send a proposal to the
CLOSER secretariat Workshop chairs and Special Session chairs will
benefit from logistics support and other types of support including
secretariat and financial support to facilitate the development of a
valid idea


Should you have any question please feel free to contact me


Kind regards
Jose Marques

Begin forwarded message

From Takayuki Ito <itotakayuki@nitechacjp
Date  November   AM GMT
To agents@csumbcedu
 agents CALL FOR PROPOSALS  Agents and MultiAgent Systems Schools


CALL FOR PROPOSALS AGENT and MULTIAGENT SYSTEM SCHOOLS


The International Foundation for Autonomous Agents and Multiagent Systems
IFAAMAS invites proposals for Agent and Multiagent System Schools from
countries or regions that have been traditionally underrepresented in the AAMAS
conference International Joint Conference on Autonomous Agents and Multiagent
Systems For more information on the conference series please look at
wwwaamasconferenceorg

The intent is to encourage further participation of researchers from such
countries in AAMAS and to foster research in the field of agent and multiagent
systems Attendees at such schools can be from academia typically graduate
students but also faculty looking to enter the field or from industry and
government

WHAT IS IFAAMAS?

IFAAMAS is the International Foundation for Autonomous Agents and Multiagent
Systems httpifaamasorg It is a legally registered notforprofit
organisation responsible for organising the AAMAS conference series Broadly
the aims of IFAAMAS are to promote research into and awareness of agent and
multiagent systems primarily by means of its involvement in organising the
AAMAS conferences but also by providing student travel scholarships and the like

WHAT IS IFAAMAS TRYING TO ACHIEVE WITH THIS INITIATIVE?

A number of advanced schools on agent systems have been held throughout the
world since  AgentLink schools in Europe the Americas schools the Pacific
Rim region school While these events have been enormously successful they
have primarily been focussed around regions and countries that already have
substantial agent research communities and that in addition have the resources
to travel to international conferences For this reason IFAAMAS has initiated
similar teaching events in regions that are not so well represented in terms of
established research groups and that do not have easy access to funds for
international travel

WHAT KIND OF EVENTS ARE WE AIMING AT?

IFAAMAS will consider any reasonable proposal for a training event but
typically  to  days of intensive courses or tutorials presented by
internationally or regionally recognised speakers on a variety of topics in the
agent systems area with some  courses each of  day to a day duration
The aim is usually to provide both introductory and more advanced courses and in
addition to provide a "balanced curriculum" insofar as this is possible Please
do not feel constrained by this model however; IFAAMAS will consider any
reasonable structure provided a justification is given

WHAT SUPPORT WILL BE AVAILABLE?

IFAAMAS will provide a grant to subsidize the agent school so as to make it
affordable to the participants in particular by providing travel support but
not honorarium to internationally or regionally wellrecognized lecturers in
the arena of agents and multiagent systems  In the past levels of financial
support have been in the form of a roughly $ to $ grant

WHICH REGIONSCOUNTRIES ARE ELIGIBLE?

Broadly regionscountries that i do not have major established research
groups in the agents area and ii do not have easy access to funds for
international travel

HOW DO I APPLY?

Proposal writers are encouraged to submit proposals as soon as possible but no
later than November   Proposals will undergo an evaluation and
selection process Please send your proposals in plain text form to Takayuki Ito
itotakayuki@nitechacjp Proposals should include the following information

 Is there significant interest in agents and multiagent systems in the region
you plan to hold your school and will there be significant attendance at the
school?

 What structure do you envisage the event having? How many courseslecturers?
How many parallel sessions if any? Not all lecturers need be international
lecturers; including some localregional speakers can sometimes be beneficial

 Is there potential for other support sponsorship for the school beyond
IFAAMAS? For instance would some universities industry or the government
potentially support the school?

 Can you give a preliminary breakdown of costs? Note that a detailed
breakdown is not necessary at this stage

 When will the school be held and what will be the duration of the school?
Please provide multiple possibilities

 What is the location of the school and will this be easily accessible to
lecturers and students?

 Will affordable student accommodation be available? If so how many rooms and
how much will they cost?

 How many students might be expected to attend?

 What is the "catchment area" for your school ie which countriesregions
might you expect students from and what proportion will be from
underrepresented countries?


IFAAMAS Education and Training Subcommittee

Takayuki Ito Nagoya Institute of Technology Japan chair
Michael Luck King's College London UK
Kate Larson University of Waterloo Canada



Takayuki Ito
 Associate Professor School of TechnoBusiness Administration Dept of

  PhD positions  reserved for women in Computational Logic at
 the Vienna University of Technology
BODY Dear colleagues

The Vienna University of Technology is offering  PhD Positions   of
them reserved for female applicants   for the  doctoral program
"Mathematical Logic in Computer Science" to be given no later than
March 
We are looking for talented female students that may be interested in
pursuing this PhD Please help us spread the call

The application is already open more information below

Best regards

 Magdalena Ortiz




The Vienna University of Technology TU Wien is offering  PhD
student positions within the doctoral program

             "Mathematical Logic in Computer Science"

which is launched in Fall ; five of the positions are reserved for
female applicants

The program is jointly organized by the faculties of Informatics
Mathematics and Physics with a strong emphasis on Logic in Computer
Science; computational logic is one of the priority research areas of
the Faculty of Informatics

TU Wien has a strong international reputation in various fields
targeted in the program including

    Logic in Databases
    Computer Aided Verification
    Constraint Satisfaction and Satisfiability
    Knowledge Representation and Reasoning
    Finite Model Theory
    Quantum Information and Recursion Theory
    Proof Theory and Automated Deduction
    Many Valued and Fuzzy Logic
    Complexity Theory
    Set Theory

The program is interdisciplinary and fosters the application of
Mathematical Logic to Computer Science; two envisaged key application
areas are

    ModelBased Design and Verification
    Advanced Information Systems

The faculty of the program consists of M Baaz A Ciabattoni
T Eiter coordinator M Goldstern G Gottlob associated
A Leitsch R Pichler K Svozil S Szeider H Veith and
S Woltran

Candidates must have an MSc or equivalent degree in
Computer Science Mathematics or related fields and an excellent
record of study They should have solid basic knowledge in logic
discrete mathematics and computer science; knowledge in
fields targeted in the program is desired

Each PhD student position is funded for three years regular
employment contract with full social benefits The yearly salary ranges
from a minimum of  Euro to  Euro before taxes depending
on cofunding via associated projects

Applications are solicited starting immediately and will be
considered starting from September   until all positions are
filled but no longer than March  

Further details about the program and the application procedure are
available at httpwwwdbaituwienacatdrkolleg

For additional information please send email to
dkinfo@dbaituwienacat

   CONIELECOMP CFP

 st International Conference on Electronics Communications and Compu
ters

 CONIELECOMP 



 February thMarch nd

 Cholula Puebla MExico



 The st International Conference on Electronics Communications and
 Computers CONIELECOMP  is organized by the Department of
 Computer Sciences Electronics and Mechatronics at Universidad de las
 AmEricasPuebla MExico and cosponsored by Center for Research i
n
 Information and Automation Technologies of the Universidad de las
 AmEricas and IEEE Section Puebla CONIELECOMP will be held in Cholul
a
 Puebla MExico from February th to March nd 



 ABOUT THE CONFERENCE

 The aim of CONIELECOMP is to provide a forum for scientists and
 engineers throughout the world to present and exchange ideas and
 results from original research and applications in the listed
 technical areas but not restricted to them The first CONIELECOMP took
 place in  and it has been held annually since then The conference
 will feature keynote speakers tutorial presentations lectures and
 poster sessions



 CALL FOR PAPERS

 Prospective authors are invited to submit a  pages full paper of
 their contributions for the proceedings Once the submitted papers are
 reviewed and accepted they will be placed into the conference
 schedule The preliminary program will appear in the conference
 website Deadlines for all submissions are shown below All
 submissions will be handled electronically The CONIELECOMP 
 website httpwwwconielecomporg will provide details regarding
 paper submission registration program events accommodations and
 tourist attractions



 IMPORTANT DEADLINES

 Paper Submission A A A A A A A A A A A AOctob
er  

 Notification of acceptance A A A A A A ANovember  


 Advanced registration deadline A A A A AJanuary

AmEricasPuebla MExico and cosponsored by Center for Research in
Information and Automation Technologies of the Universidad de las
AmEricas and IEEE Section Puebla CONIELECOMP will be held in Cholula
Puebla MExico from February th to March nd 



ABOUT THE CONFERENCE

The aim of CONIELECOMP is to provide a forum for scientists and
engineers throughout the world to present and exchange ideas and
results from original research and applications in the listed
technical areas but not restricted to them The first CONIELECOMP took
place in  and it has been held annually since then The conference
will feature keynote speakers tutorial presentations lectures and
poster sessions



CALL FOR PAPERS

Prospective authors are invited to submit a  pages full paper of
their contributions for the proceedings Once the submitted papers are
reviewed and accepted they will be placed into the conference
schedule The preliminary program will appear in the conference
website Deadlines for all submissions are shown below All
submissions will be handled electronically The CONIELECOMP 
website httpwwwconielecomporg will provide details regarding
paper submission registration program events accommodations and
tourist attractions

 automata celular universal mas pequenio
BODY Estimados colaboradores amigos e interesados en automata celular

Bueno despues de empezar a elaborar un articulo sobre automata
celular y particularmente sobre la universalidad de la Regla  diez
anios atras El articulo fue dedicado para reproducir un resultado
importante en la teoria de automata celular y en teoria de la
computacion que fue presentando inicialmente en el libro "A New Kid
of Science" de Stephen Wolfram

httpwwwwolframsciencecomnksonlinetochtml

El articulo "reproduce" una maquina de Turing equivalente en el
automata celular mas pequenio demostrado ser universal sin usar
Mathematica y que es precisamente el automata celular elemental
Regla  Un repositorio general acerca de la Regla  puede ser
consultarlo desde

httpuncompuweacukgenaroRulehtml

El resultado fue desarrollado y obtenido originalmente por Matthew
Cook y la implementacion fue realizada sobre millones de celulas
usando Mathematica en un nuevo mecanismo computacional conocido como
"sistemas tag ciclicos" una variante de los ya conocidos "sistemas
tag" de Emil Post Que actualmente ademas ha ayudado al desarrollo
nuevas y mas pequenias maquinas de Turing

httpwwwcomplexsystemscomArchivehierarchyabstractcgi?vol&iss&art

El articulo se empezo a realizar desde el anio  en el Departamento
de Microcomputadoras de la UAP motivado guiado e inspirado
indudablmente por el Prof Harold V McIntosh desde su articulo "Rule
 Is Universal A Gamin's Guide To Goldbergean Gadgeteering"
Finalmente despues de enviarlo al Journal of Cellular Automata en el
 ha aparecido en el numero destinado para el 

Los resultados de esta investigacion inducieron intrevistas y
discusiones personales tanto con Wolfram y Cook anios atras en
Estados Unidos y Zurich respectivamente entre otros expertos en
automata celular y computacion como fueron Martin Davis y Kenichi
Morita

httpwwwoldcitypublishingcomJCAJCAcontentsJCAvncontentshtml

Creemos que puede ser de su interes y no queremos dejar pasar esta
oportunidad para compartirles acerca de la publicacion del articulo
Deseamos que resulte ser interesante para ustedes investigadores y
estudiantes

La version en PDF antes de ser publicado se encuentra disponible desde

httpuncompuweacukgenaroPapersPapers_on_CA_filesrepCTSRpdf

Saludos
Genaro


 
Genaro Juarez Martinez
Unconventional Computing Centre UWE UK
httpuncompuweacukgenaro

 Fwd CFP ICCC
BODY CALL FOR PAPERS ICCC

nd International Conference on Computational Creativity
April  
Mexico City Mexico
httpiccccuauammx

Original contributions are solicited in all areas related to
Computational Creativity including but not limited to

AA  computational paradigms for understanding creativity including
heuristic search analogicalA and metalevel reasoning and
rerepresentation;
AA  metrics frameworks and formalizations for the evaluation of
creativity in computational systems note quasiformal approaches
that for example argue for recognition without definition or that
define the absence of creativity may have interesting implications for
computational creativity;
AA  perspectives on computational creativity including philosophy
models of cognition and human behavior and intelligent systems;
AA  development and assessment of computational creativitysupport to
ols;
AA  creativityoriented computing in learning teaching and other
aspects of education;
AA  innovation improvisation and related pursuits investigating the
production of novel experiences and artifacts within a computational
framework;
AA  computational accounts of factors that enhance creativity
including emotion surprise unexpectedness conflict diversity
motivation knowledge intuition reward structures and technologies
eg modeling simulation humanintheloop humanmachine
collaboration etc;
AA  computational treatment of social aspects of creativity
including the relationship between individual and social creativity
diffusion of ideas collaboration and creativity formation of
creative teams and creativity in social settings eg modeling
simulation humanintheloop humanmachine collaboration etc;
AA  specific applications with a computational component to music
language narrative poetry the arts architecture entertainment
mathematical and scientific discovery programming andor design;
AA  detailed system descriptions of creative systems including
engineering difficulties faced example sessions and artifacts
produced and applications of the system;
AA  domainspecific vs generalized creativity  does the domain
of study affect the perception of creativity?A Are there general
computational creative principles that can be applied across domains?

PAPERS

We invite papers that make a scientific contribution to the field of
computational creativity and report work that involves computation
eg fully autonomous systems modeling support for human
creativity simulation humanmachine collaboration etc

We welcome studies of human creativity that in some way propose a
computational model for that creativity

When papers report on creative computer systems we particularly
encourage them to discuss systems having general or at least multiple
sorts of results to detail the methods used to design and develop the
system or to include useful related theoretical discussion

We invite papers that go beyond simply documenting interesting systems
to describe advances in cognitive science assessment methods design
methods or other research areas

DEMOSARTS SHOW AND TELL

We invite proposals for demonstrations of computational systems
exhibiting behavior that would be deemed creative in humans and for
the exhibition of artifacts created using computational means either
primarily or as support for a human creator

More information will soon be available at httpiccccuauammx
Or send email to iccc@correocuauammx

IMPORTANT DATES

December    Submission deadline
February    Authors' Notification
March    Deadline for final cameraready copies
April    ICCC in Mexico City

?	Intrusion detection
?	Protocol verification
?	Protocol repair
?	Security policy specification and enforcement Information flow control
?	Web  applications

Publication

Papers will be published in English in the main proceedings of the MICAI
workshop
Authors of accepted papers will be invited to submit an extended version
of their papers for a possible publication in a special issue of a journal
We also welcome papers accepted in the MICAI conference for people interested
in obtaining additional feedback and access to a specialised audience

Submissions

We invite interested members of the scientific community to submit a tenpage
paper reporting on novel original work possibly in progress where artificial
intelligence or a statistical method is applied to solve problems of computer
security

Submissions should be uploaded in PDF format through the workshop submission
web page

Paper format

Please use the LaTeX style file provided by Springer for the LLNCS series
httpwwwspringeronlinecomlncs Each submission should include the names
and complete addresses including email of all authors Correspondence will
be sent to the first author unless otherwise indicated All papers must
be submitted in English

Presentations

Each workshop attendee will be allocated a minute slot for a short talk
to introduce his research work

Organisers

The workshop is being organised by two research groups in computer security
at Tecnológico de Monterrey one is based in Monterrey httpspeechmtyitesmmxcybersecurity
and the other in Estado de Mexico httphomepagecemitesmmxraulmnetsec

Contact

Please email wsec@easychairorg should you have any queries about the
 MICAI Workshop in Computer Security

Please visit our site httpcnapcemitesmmxWSEC for more information

                    CALL FOR PAPERS

  LogicLanguages Algorithms and New Methods of Reasoning LANMR'

   WORKSHOP OVERVIEW 
  
  The Logic and Computation Mexican Group invites you to participate in the
sixth Latin American Workshop on New Methods of 
  Reasoning to be held in November from th to th  at the Facultad
de Ciencias Fisico Matematicas Benemerita Universidad 
  Autonoma de Puebla BUAP in Puebla Pue Mexico
  
  The proceedings of LANMR' will be published in CEUR Workshop Proceedings
CEURWSorg that is a publication service of Sun 
  SITE Central Europe operated by RWTH Aachen University with the support of
Tilburg University CEURWSorg is recognized as a 
  publication series by Deutsche Bibliothek ISSN 
  
  Suggested topics include but are not limited to
  
   Logic programming and nonmonotonic reasoning
   Algorithms applied to logic
   Answer Set Programming
   Knowledge representation
   Belief representation
   Paraconsistent logics
   Deduction techniques
   Automated reasoning
   Nonclassical logics
   Reasoning about situations and actions
   Planning
   Algorithms for graph theory in AI
   Multiagent systems
   Preferences
   Default and abductive reasoning
   Wellfounded semantics
   Cognitive agents
   Novel applications
   Natural language
   Argumentation
  
  It is expected a relation to Logic in the submitted papers
  
  A selection of extended workshop papers will be published in a
  special issue
  
  
  
  
   INVITED SPEAKER 
  
  
  Prof Dr Torsten Schaub Institut UTF?fï¿½r Informatik
  UTF?Universitï¿½t Potsdam Germany
  
  Received his diploma and dissertation in informatics in  and 
  respectively from the TechnicalUniversity of Darmstadt Germany 
  He received his habilitation in informatics in  from the University 
  of Rennes I France From  to  he was a Researcher at the 
  Technical University at Darmstadt From  to  he was a 
  Research Associate at IRISAINRIA at Rennes From  to  
  he was University Professor at the University of Angers At Angers
  he founded the researchgroup FLUX dealing with the automatisation
  of reasoning from incomplete contradictory and evolutive information
  Since  he is University Professor for knowledge processing
  and information systems at the University of Potsdam In  he became
  Adjunct Professor at the School of Computing Science at Simon
  Fraser University Canada; and since  he is also an Adjunct
  Professor in the Institute for Integrated and Intelligent Systems at
  Griffiths University Australia His research interests range from t
  he theoretic foundations to the practical implementation of methods
  for reasoning from incomplete andor inconsistent information in
  particular Answer set programming
  
  Email torsten@csunipotsdamde 
  httpwwwcsunipotsdamde~torsten
  
  
  
   SUBMISSION 
  
  
  Papers should be written in  English  and  formatted 
  according  to the  LNCS style and not exceed  pages
  including references and figures Submitted papers 
  will be  to a doubleblind review process To submit a paper 
  the authors should send an email with  "LANMR Submission" 
  toosoriomauri@gmailcom and czepedac@gmailcom with the PDF 
  file of the paper as an attachment and the following  information 
  in plain text in the body of the email 
  
   Paper title
   Author names
   email
   A short abstract
   Up to five keywords

 Call for Papers CCE 
BODY Dear Professor Student and Professional

On behalf of the Organizing Committee of the  th International
Conference on Electrical Engineering Computing Science and Automatic
Control CCE  Formerly known as ICEEE we are pleased to invite
you to participate in this event by submitting original technical
articles not included in other conference
This event is sponsored by the Electron Device Society EDS of the
Institute of Electrical and Electronics Engineers IEEE in which the
Conference Proceedings edition has registered both ISBN and IEEE Catalog
numbers

Location Tuxtla Gutiérrez Chiapas Mexico
Conference September  

Important Dates
Submission of manuscripts May  
Notification of acceptancerejection June  
Final revised manuscripts July  
Tutorial Courses September  

Topics of interest include but are not limited to
 Automatic Control
 Biomedical Enginnering
 Communications systems
 Computer science and Computer Engineering
 Mechatronics
 Solidstate materials electron devices and integrated circuits

The complete information of this academic and scientific conference can
be found at the conference’s site

httpccecinvestavmx

The authors of the best papers presented at the conference will be
contacted after the event for submitting extended versions of their
works for possible inclusion in a book to be published in English

We would highly appreciate it if you could resend this invitation to any
of your colleagues who might be interested in this event

If you received this email in error please forward it to the
appropriate department at your institution If you wish to unsubscribe
please send an email to cce@cinvestavmx include unsubscribe in the 

Sincerely


Dr José Antonio Moreno Cadenas
Dr Carlos Coello Coello
Dr Alexander Poznyak Gorbatch
General Chairs CCE 

We apologize if you receive this message more than once

Av Instituto Politécnico Nacional No Col San Pedro Zacatenco CP
 México D F
Teléfono  ext  Fax 
email cce@cinvestavmx httpccecinvestavmx


Estimado a Colega

Los departamentos de Ingeniería Eléctrica Control Automático y
Computación del CINVESTAVIPN invitan a la comunidad científica y a
los profesionales de la ingeniería a participar en la

th International Conference on Electrical Engineering Computing
Science and Automatic Control CCE Formerly known as ICEEE

Los dias   y  de Septiembre de  en la Ciudad de Tuxtla
Gutiérrez Chiapas México

Esta congreso tiene como objetivo promover la vinculación entre los
sectores productivo y académico del país ofreciendo a estudiantes
investigadores y profesionistas un foro propicio para presentar e
informarse de los avances y nuevos desarrollos realizados en Ingeniería
Eléctrica Electrónica Computación Control Automático y áreas afines
El evento comprende la presentación de ponencias libres así como de
conferencias plenarias ofrecidas por invitados tanto nacionales como
extranjeros de reconocido prestigio Así mismo los días  y  de
Septiembre se ofrecerán varios cursos como preámbulo de este importante
evento Para mayor información por favor visite nuestra página
httpccecinvestavmx

Se aceptarán ponencias originales y que no hayan sido publicadas en otro
congreso en cualquiera de las siguientes áreas Ciencias de la
Computación Ingeniería en Computación Comunicaciones Control
Automático Bioelectrónica Biomedicina Mecatrónica Electrónica del
Estado Sólido Semiconductores Sensores y Actuadores Sistemas de
Potencia entre otros

Los trabajos serán evaluados por un Comité Técnico formado por expertos

BODY 
  Programa para el establecimiento de vínculos de investigación de
  América del Norte

El Programa para el Establecimiento de Vínculos de Investigación de 
América del Norte fue diseñado para facilitar la colaboración 
norteamericana al interior de la comunidad académica Su objetivo es 
promover el desarrollo de redes de intercambio permanentes al 
proporcionar ayuda a los equipos de investigadores de Canadá Estados 
Unidos y México en la organización de seminarios talleres y otras 
formas de establecer vínculos de investigación

El Ministerio de Asuntos Exteriores y Comercio Internacional de Canadá 
ofrecerá apoyos de $ dólares canadienses     o hasta $ 
dólares canadienses cuando se demuestran financiamientos externos Los 
apoyos son para ayudar al establecimiento o el desarrollo de redes de 
investigación en América del Norte

Las solicitudes serán tomadas en consideración de acuerdo con los 
procedimientos directrices y condiciones que se describen en las 
páginas siguientes

     Detalles completos y formularios Únicamente en inglés
      <httpwwwinternationalgccastudiesetudesnarlppnarraspx?langeng
      y francés
      <httpwwwinternationalgccastudiesetudesnarlppnarraspx?langfra


httpwwwinternationalgccastudiesetudesnarlppnarraspx?langen

La recepción de solicitudes está a cargo de

Pierre Sved
Coordinador de Asuntos Académicos
Embajada de Canadá en México
pierresved@internationalgcca

 diagrams Multimedia Grand Challenge  Call for Participation
BODY 
                           CALL FOR PARTICIPATION
                        Multimedia Grand Challenge
                  httpwwwmultimediagrandchallengecom
                        
                            ACM Multimedia  
                    October th  Firenze Italy
                           httpwwwacmmmorg


What problems do Google Yahoo HP Radvision CeWe Nokia and other companies see driving the future of multimedia? The Multimedia Grand Challenge is a set of problems and issues from these industry leaders geared to engage the Multimedia research community towards solving relevant interesting and challenging questions in the multimedia industry�s  year horizon The Grand Challenge was first presented as part of ACM Multimedia  and it will be presented again in slightly modified form at ACM Multimedia  Researchers are encouraged to submit working systems in response to these challenges to win the grand Challenge competition



Challenges

CeWe       Photo Set Theme Identification
Google     Personal Diaries
Google     Video Genre Classification
HP         Visual Communication
Nokia      Photo Location & Orientation
Radvision  Content Adaptation
Radvision  VideoConf Experience
Yahoo     Novel Image Understanding
Yahoo     Video Segmentation

We encourage you to consider the challenges and submit your contribution to the ACM Multimedia  Grand Challenge track The top submissions will be presented in a special event during the ACM Multimedia  conference in Florence Italy Based on these oral presentations in Florence winners will be selected for Grand Challenge awards worth  USD



Paper Submission

New in  _any_ long short or demo paper submitted to the regular ACM Multimedia conference can be considered for the Grand Challenge Regular papers that want to be considered should submit a page additional statement indicating why this work addresses a certain challenge best In addition papers demonstrations and ideas that do not fit the normal scientific style may be submitted to the Grand Challenge by submitting a separate page paper to the Grand Challenge only We are afraid that we will NOT consider papers in this path that have been rejected for the scientific program

A page statement to accompany an _accepted_ paper or a new page grand challenge paper should be prepared in doublecolumn ACM proceedings style and submitted via httpedasinfoN 

The submissions must
o Significantly address one of the industry challenges posted on the Grand Challenge web site
o Depict working presentable systems or demos
o Describe why the system presents a novel and interesting solution

A number of solutions perhaps  will be selected as finalists and invited to describe their work demonstrate their solution and argue for the paper's success in the Grand Challenge Session in Florence  Each finalist will have several minutes to present their case  Final winners will be chosen by industry scientists engineers and business luminaries



Key Dates

August   Submission deadline
September   Acceptance notification
October   Conference starts



Contact

Malcolm Slaney Yahoo Research USA malcolm@ieeeorg
Cees Snoek University of Amsterdam The Netherlands cgmsnoek@uvanl

BODY México D F a  de marzo de 

Circular 

Estimadoa colega

Informo a usted que las siguientes convocatorias de la Academia Mexicana 
de Ciencias AMC se encuentran vigentes y pueden ser consultadas en la 
página electrónica de la AMC wwwamcunammx



 Admisión de nuevos miembros regulares 

 Premios de Investigación  para Científicos Jóvenes

 Becas para las Mujeres en la Ciencia L´OréalUNESCOAMC



 La convocatoria de Admisión de nuevos miembros regulares tiene como 
fecha límite para presentar candidatos el  de junio de 

 Considerada como la distinción más importante que confiere la 
Academia los Premios de Investigación se otorgan a jóvenes 
investigadores en el caso de los hombres menores de  años y de las 
mujeres  años que realicen investigación de punta en las áreas de 
Ciencias Exactas Naturales Sociales Humanidades y en Ingeniería y 
Tecnología la fecha límite para registrar candidatos es el  de mayo 
de 

 La AMC L´Oréal México la Comisión Mexicana de Cooperación con la 
UNESCO CONALMEX y la Oficina de la UNESCO en México instituyeron las 
“Becas para Mujeres en la Ciencia L’Oréal–UNESCOAMC” con el objetivo 
de promover la participación de las mujeres en la ciencia para la 
realización de estudios científicos avanzados en universidades u otras 
instituciones mexicanas reconocidas Las participantes deben ser 
mexicanas menores de  años y haber concluido el doctorado en los 
últimos cinco años esta convocatoria cierra el lunes  de mayo de 

En virtud de la importancia que estas convocatorias tienen para la vida 
académica de nuestra comunidad mucho agradeceré la difusión que pueda 
hacer de las mismas

Agradezco su amable atención y aprovecho la oportunidad para enviarle un 
cordial saludo

Atentamente

Dra Rosaura Ruiz Gutiérrez
Presidenta
Academia Mexicana de Ciencias

ConstraintHandling in Evolutionary Optimization editado por Efrén 
MezuraMontes Studies in Computational Intelligence Series Vol  
Springer 

Este libro editado en el Laboratorio Nacional de Informática Avanzada 
LANIA AC presenta los avances más recientes en el uso y adaptación de 
algoritmos evolutivos y de inteligencia colectiva para resolver problemas 
de optimización numérica en presencia de restricciones El libro está 
dirigido a investigadores y estudiantes en disciplinas como optimización 
inteligencia artificial investigación de operaciones ingeniería y ciencia 
de la computación La página del libro es la siguiente

httpwwwspringercomengineeringbook

                    Unete a la Red Tematica en Robótica

La Robótica es un área científica y tecnológica estratégica con
enorme crecimiento e impacto tanto actualmente como en el futuro
La revolución Robótica va a detonar importantes avances científicos y
tecnológicos en diversas áreas como la Mecánica la Electrónica el
Control Automático y la Computación; ayudará a resolver problemas
importantes en seguridad salud medio ambiente y productividad entre
otros; y creará una nueva industria con un importante impacto
económico En su conjunto la Robótica impulsará el desarrollo de los
países que adopten esta tecnología Un grupo importante de investigadores
esta convencido de que es necesario impulsar de manera coordinada
la Robótica en México Para tal fin se está sometiendo una solicitud de
creación de una Red Temática en Robótica aprovechando la convocatoria
de creación de nuevas redes temáticas de Conacyt

El Objetivo General de esta Red es impulsar el desarrollo de la Robótica
en México incluyendo investigación educación desarrollo tecnológico
y formación de empresas; así como sus aplicaciones que ayuden a
resolver problemas nacionales y fomenten el desarrollo económico del país

Dentro de los objetivos específicos se tienen

 Realizar un censo nacional del estado de la Robótica en el país
 Fomentar la educación y difusión de la Robótica en México
 Impulsar y facilitar el desarrollo de proyectos nacionales insignia
   en Robótica con carácter interinstitucional y multidisciplinario
 Identificar las principales aplicaciones de la Robótica en el país
   e impulsar proyectos en estas áreas
 Fomentar la colaboración academiaindustria y la colaboración
   internacional
 Impulsar la puesta en operación de un centro o instituto nacional de
   robótica

Si estas interesado en participar en este esfuerzo te pedimos que
mandes la siguiente informacion A MAS TARDAR ESTE VIERNES a
Manlio Barajas manlito@gmailcom con copia a José Luis Gordillo 
JLGordillo@itesmmx
 Nombre completo
 Nombre de tu institución
 Número de registro de CVU
 Resumen de tu CV de maximo un parrafo

 AMPLN CLEFLab on Plagiarism Detection and Wikipedia Vandalism Detection
 PAN'
BODY 


Call for Participation
Evaluation Campaign on Plagiarism Detection and Wikipedia Vandalism
Detection




           held in conjunction with the CLEF' conference
                  in Padua Italy September 
                         httppanwebisde




About the Campaign




Plagiarism detection in text documents is a challenging retrieval task
today's detection systems are faced with intricate situations such as
obfuscated plagiarism or plagiarism within and across languages
Moreover the source of a plagiarism case may be hidden in a large
collection of documents or it may not be available at all Informally
the respective CLEFLab task can be described as follows

  Plagiarism Detection Given a set of suspicious documents and a set
    of source documents the task is to find all plagiarized sections
    in the suspicious documents and if available the corresponding
    source sections

Following the success of the  campaign and based on our experience
we will provide a revised evaluation corpus consisting of artificial and
simulated plagiarism


Vandalism has always been one of Wikipedia's biggest problems However
the detection of vandalism is done mostly manually by volunteers and
research on automatic vandalism detection is still in its infancy
Hence solutions are to be developed which aid Wikipedians in their
efforts Informally the respective CLEFLab task can be described as
follows

  Wikipedia Vandalism Detection Given a set of edits on Wikipedia
    articles the task is to identify all edits which are vandalism
    ie all edits whose editors had bad intentions


Participants are invited to submit results for one or both of the tasks





Important Dates




open              Registration
Mar        Training corpora release
                  Preliminary training corpora are alread available
May        Test corpora release
Jun        Result submission deadline
Jun        Notification of performance
Jul        Paper submission deadline
Aug        Notification of reviews
Sep        Final paper deadline
Sep     Evaluation lab at CLEF conference

CALL FOR PAPERS POSTERS AND WORKSHOPS
Paper Abstracts optional  December 
Papers full   pages  January 
Posters abstracts  February 
Workshop proposals  February 

This biennial conference series provides an international forum for
the presentation and discussion of stateoftheart and cuttingedge
design research with a focus on artificial intelligence cognitive
science and computational theories in design The conference
proceedings will form a continuing archive of design computing and
cognition research The conference will be preceded by a series of
halfday workshops on specialist topics in design computing and
cognition

A set of research papers that have been refereed by an international
board of reviewers will be presented and published as a book Posters
describing ongoing research will be presented

Details at httpmasongmuedu~jgeroconferencesdcc

CALL FOR PAPERS


                       Artificial Life XII

               The Twelfth International Conference
        on the Synthesis and Simulation of Living Systems

            th  rd August  Odense Denmark

                     httpwwwalifexiiorg



You are invited to submit papers to the upcoming Twelfth International
Conference on Artificial Life Please forward this call responsibly

IMPORTANT DATES
      February  Full paperabstract submission deadline
      April  Notice of acceptance for full papers
      May  Camera ready deadline
      August  Conference dates

OVERVIEW
It is a great pleasure for the Center for Fundamental Living Technology
FLinT at University of Southern Denmark SDU to host the th
International Conference on Artificial Life

The conference will be organized around the theme of identifying and
synthesizing the critical properties of living and lifelike systems
eg selfreplication selfassembly selforganization metabolism
adaptation evolution The meeting will reflect all of the main areas
of artificial life research including wet systems based on carbon
chemistry soft systems realized just in software and hard 
systems
consisting of autonomous robotic agents as well as a variety of social
and technical systems that embody the critical properties of living
systems The conference will have broad interdisciplinary interest
because living processes are found virtually everywhere

It has been a decade since the last organized effort to identify the
key open problems in artificial life So another important goal of
the workshop is to review progress on the open problems and reevaluate
what are the key open problems today

Some sessions in the conference will be devoted to detailed discussion
of specific s We envision a variety of smaller forums which
will address such topics as the chemistry of assembling protocells
the energetics and mechanical implementation of robots or software
and social issues for collective intelligence platforms In addition
a poster session will give the opportunity to discuss selected works
peertopeer In this manner we hope the conference can increase both
the depth and breath of the scientific work presented

The conference will be held in Odense one of the oldest cities of
Denmark As Denmark's thirdlargest city it offers a mixture of
nightlife beautiful streetscapes great shopping opportunities and
a rich cultural heritage

Prospective participants will have four tracks for participating in
the conference
    submitting a paper to be presented at the conference
      and published in the conference proceedings
      tentatively to be published by MIT Press
    submitting an abstract for a presentation or poster at
      the conference
    proposing a conference session of a number of people
      presenting work on a specific 
    proposing a selforganized satellite workshops which
      would take place immediately before during or immediately
      after the conference

All submissions will be  to peer review and submissions to
tracks  and  have an equal chance of being accepted as presentations
Revised and expanded versions of excellent presentations at the
conference will be placed on a fasttrack for submission to the
Artificial Life journal

Please stay tuned for the call for conference submissions and submission
deadlines

PAPERABSTRACT FORMAT
There are two options for submission either full paper format or
abstract format Full papers have an  page maximum length while
abstracts are limited to two pages Graphics and figures are
encouraged Every submission will be  to full peer review
All accepted submissions will be allocated an oral presentation slot
or poster with no distinction being made between the two submission
formats

For proposed conference sessions and satellite workshops a onepage
abstract needs to be submitted for peer review Please note that all
presentations in proposed conference sessions will undergo peer review
All formatting guidelines including word and latex style files and
submission instructions will be available on the conference submission
page

PUBLICATION
Every accepted fullpaper and abstract submission will be published
by MIT Press in a single online openaccess proceedings volume In
addition the best  papers will have the opportunity to be
published in special issues of the MIT Press journal Artificial Life

ORGANIZATION
Steen Rasmussen chair Lone Ladegaard administrative chair
Martin Hanczyc PierreAlain Monnard Kasper StFy Daniel Merkle
Harold Fellermann Mark DFrr Sarah Maurer

HOST INSTITUTION
FLinT Center for Fundamental Living Technology
Department of Physics and Chemistry
University of Southern Denmark
Odense Denmark

CONTACT
For further information about the conference program travel
accommodation and local arrangements please see
httpwwwalifexiiorg  For questions about the submission
and reviewing process please email submissions@alifexiiorg
For all other questions contact questions@alifexiiorg
_______________________________________________
ALifeXII@sdudk
httpwwwALifeXIIorg

              Special Track on Uncertain Reasoning UR
                  
                 httpwwwiritfr~LaurentPerrusselur

                              FLAIRS
                    Daytona Beach Florida USA 
                           May  
  
                           Call For Papers 


Many problems in AI in reasoning planning learning perception and 
robotics require the agent to operate with incomplete or uncertain 
information The objective of this track is to a present and discusses 
a broad and diverse range of current work on uncertain reasoning 
including theoretical and applied research based on different
paradigms 
We hope that the variety and richness of this track will help to
promote 
cross fertilization among the different approaches for uncertain
reasoning 
and in this way foster the development of new ideas and paradigms

The Special Track on Uncertain Reasoning UR is the oldest track in
FLAIRS conferences running annually since  The UR' Special
Track at the nd International Florida Artificial Intelligence Research
Society Conference FLAIRS is the th in the series As the past
tracks  UR' seeks to bring together researchers working on broad
issues related to reasoning under uncertainty 

Invited Speaker

Prof David Poole will give a keynote speech during the special track 
Professor Poole is in the Department of Computer Science Univ of 
British Columbia Canada He is a member of the Laboratory for 
Computational Intelligence and a Fellow of the Association for 
the Advancement of Artificial Intelligence His main research interests 
are artificial intelligence intelligent agents knowledge
representation 
and reasoning under uncertainty A tentative title of his talk is
"What should the WorldWide Mind believe? Knowledge and uncertainty at a
global scale"
  
Scope

Papers on all aspects of uncertain reasoning are invited Papers of 
particular interest include but are not limited to

     Uncertain reasoning formalisms calculi and methodologies
     Reasoning with probability possibility fuzzy logic 
		belief function vagueness granularity rough sets 
		and probability logics
     Modeling and reasoning using imprecise and indeterminate 
	  information such as 
		Choquet capacities comparative orderings convex sets 
		of measures and intervalvalued probabilities
     Exact approximate and qualitative uncertain reasoning
     Graphical models of uncertainty
     Multiagent uncertain reasoning and decision making
     Decisiontheoretic planning and Markov decision process
     Temporal reasoning and uncertainty
     Epistemic logics
     Argumentation
     Belief change and Merging
     Nonmonotonic and conditional Logics
     Similaritybased reasoning
     Construction of models from elicitation data mining and 
		knowledge discovery
     Uncertain reasoning in information retrieval filtering fusion
		diagnosis prediction situation assessment
     Practical applications of uncertain reasoning


Paper Submission and Publication

Submitted papers must be original and not submitted concurrently to a
journal or another conference Full papers may be up to  pages and
poster papers up to  pages Papers must be in AAAI format and
submitted as PDF through the EasyChair conference system  Instructions
on the submission procedure will be available at the UR' website

httpwwwiritfr~LaurentPerrusselur

The proceedings of FLAIRS will be published by the AAAI An author of
each accepted paper is required to register attend and present the
paper at the UR track 

The International Journal of Approximate Reasoning will publish a
special issue devoted to extended versions of the top papers at the
track

BODY Hola Luis

Te paso el texto para incluir en el boletín de Remidec en el que se da 
la noticia de la constitución de la AMPLN

Saludos
Manuel



El pasado  de octubre del presente año en las instalaciones del 
INAOE bajo el to Taller Nacional de Tecnologías de Lenguaje Humano se 
declaró formalmente constituida la Asociación Mexicana para el 
Procesamiento de Lenguaje Natural AMPLN; wwwamplnorg

La AMPLN será un catalizador que promoverá la interacción e intercambio 
de ideas entre especialistas mexicanos en el procesamiento de lenguaje 
natural PLN; y difundirá los logros y la importancia del PLN entre la 
sociedad nacional Cabe mencionar que es indispensable hacer 
investigación en PLN para ser capaces de tratar la información expresada 
en nuestro propio idioma; y sólo así estaremos en condiciones de 
responder a las exigencias de las nuevas Tecnologías de la Información y 
la Comunicación Recordemos que el idioma Español es hablado por 
aproximadamente  millones de personas y que México es el país 
hispanohablante más poblado Sin embargo la influencia hoy en día de 
nuestro idioma en la sociedad de la información es mínima 
Desgraciadamente la ciencia y la tecnología asociada al tratamiento del 
idioma Español no se ha desarrollado con el ímpetu necesario De ahí la 
importancia de la constitución de la AMPLN como medio para enfrentar el 
enorme rezago en esta área

La asociación se constituyó con la participación de  investigadores 
del área pertenecientes a las  instituciones enlistadas a 
continuación el Centro de Investigación en Computación CICIPN el 
Instituto de Investigación en Matemáticas Aplicadas y Sistemas 
IIMASUNAM el Instituto de Ingeniería IINGENUNAM la Universidad 
Autónoma Metropolitana UAMCuajimalpa el Instituto Nacional de 
Astrofísica Óptica y Electrónica INAOE la Benemérita Universidad 
Autónoma de Puebla BUAP la Universidad Autónoma de Querétaro UAQ 
la Universidad Autónoma del Estado de México UAEM el Centro Nacional 
de Investigación y Desarrollo Tecnológico CENIDET el Centro de 
Investigación y de Estudios Avanzados del Instituto Politécnico 
Nacional Unidad Tamaulipas CINVESTAVTamaulipas la Universidad 
Autónoma de Ciudad del Carmen UNACAR y la Universidad de Alabama

 
Dr Manuel Montes y Gómez
Laboratorio de Tecnologías del Lenguage
Instituto Nacional de Astrofísica Optica y Electrónica INAOE

Calle Luis Enrique Erro No

 Call for Papers  Uncertain Reasoning at FLAIRS
BODY Please redistribute sorry for duplicates Regards Enrique



              Special Track on Uncertain Reasoning UR
                  
                 httpwwwiritfr~LaurentPerrusselur

                              FLAIRS
                    Daytona Beach Florida USA 
                           May  
  
                           Call For Papers 


Many problems in AI in reasoning planning learning perception and 
robotics require the agent to operate with incomplete or uncertain 
information The objective of this track is to a present and discusses 
a broad and diverse range of current work on uncertain reasoning 
including theoretical and applied research based on different
paradigms 
We hope that the variety and richness of this track will help to
promote 
cross fertilization among the different approaches for uncertain
reasoning 
and in this way foster the development of new ideas and paradigms

The Special Track on Uncertain Reasoning UR is the oldest track in
FLAIRS conferences running annually since  The UR' Special
Track at the nd International Florida Artificial Intelligence Research
Society Conference FLAIRS is the th in the series As the past
tracks  UR' seeks to bring together researchers working on broad
issues related to reasoning under uncertainty 

Invited Speaker

Prof David Poole will give a keynote speech during the special track 
Professor Poole is in the Department of Computer Science Univ of 
British Columbia Canada He is a member of the Laboratory for 
Computational Intelligence and a Fellow of the Association for 
the Advancement of Artificial Intelligence His main research interests 
are artificial intelligence intelligent agents knowledge
representation 
and reasoning under uncertainty A tentative title of his talk is
"What should the WorldWide Mind believe? Knowledge and uncertainty at a
global scale"
  
Scope

Papers on all aspects of uncertain reasoning are invited Papers of 
particular interest include but are not limited to

     Uncertain reasoning formalisms calculi and methodologies
     Reasoning with probability possibility fuzzy logic 
		belief function vagueness granularity rough sets 
		and probability logics
     Modeling and reasoning using imprecise and indeterminate 
	  information such as 
		Choquet capacities comparative orderings convex sets 
		of measures and intervalvalued probabilities
     Exact approximate and qualitative uncertain reasoning
     Graphical models of uncertainty
     Multiagent uncertain reasoning and decision making
     Decisiontheoretic planning and Markov decision process
     Temporal reasoning and uncertainty
     Epistemic logics
     Argumentation
     Belief change and Merging
     Nonmonotonic and conditional Logics
     Similaritybased reasoning
     Construction of models from elicitation data mining and 
		knowledge discovery
     Uncertain reasoning in information retrieval filtering fusion
		diagnosis prediction situation assessment
     Practical applications of uncertain reasoning
