 Fwd Invitation ENC Track PhD Workshop
BODY 
 Please excuse us if you receive this mail more than once

 
 Call for Participation ENCB PhD workshop

 The PhD Workshop is intended to bring together PhD students 
 working on
 topics related to ENC The workshop will offer PhD students the
 opportunity to present discuss and receive feedback on their 
 research in
 a constructive and international atmosphere The workshop will be 
 attended
 by professors and researchers that will actively participate and
 contribute to the discussions The workshop is colocated with ENC 

 and
 will take place immediately before the conference

 Submission guidelines papers' submission at
 httpwwweasychairorgconferences?confDenc

 Papers describing doctoral work should be submitted in PDF 
 preferred or
 PostScript The paper length must not exceed  pages including all
 parts The paper has to be formatted according to the ENC conference
 manuscript preparation guidelines except the amount of pages which 

 is
 limited to  pages for the PhD workshop Workshop and paper 
 language is
 English In contrast to regular conference papers submissions should
 address specifically doctoral work Therefore the following 
 elements are
 recommended

        A clear formulation of the research question
        An identification of the significant problems in the field 
of
 research
        An outline of the current knowledge of the problem domain 

 as well
 as the state of existing solutions
        A presentation of any preliminary ideas the proposed 
 approach and
 the results achieved so far
        A sketch of the applied research methodology
        A description of the PhD project's contribution to the 
 problem
 solution
        A discussion of how the suggested solution is different 
 new or
 better as compared to existing approaches to the problem

 The intention of this workshop is to support and inspire PhD 
 students
 during their ongoing research efforts Therefore it is necessary that
 authors will have neither achieved their PhD degree nor submitted 

 their
 thesis before the PhD workshop September   To enforce 
 this rule
 we require authors to disclose their expected graduation date and 
 their
 advisor's name when submitting PhD students that have already 
 published
 significant parts of their work at some other major conference are
 asked to step back and offer other PhD students the opportunity to
 discuss their research topics Please note that similar to a
 PhD thesis only a single author is allowed per submission to the 

 ENC
 PhD workshop If several PhD students usually working together 

 as a
 team want to submit every team member has to submit individually 

 The
 PhD advisor is not stated as coauthor

 Important dates
        Submission deadline  September 
        Acceptance or rejection notification  September 
        Cameraready th September 

 Accepted submissions will be published in the workshop proceedings
 Participants should register for the ENC conference itself at student
 rate

 Chairs
 Maria Trinidad Serna Instituto TecnolFgico de Hermosillo MExico
 tserna@ ithmx
 Ma del Carmen Mezura Universidad Veracruzana MExico
 cmezura@uvmx

Fernando


 Hola Dr Arámbula

 Soy egresado del posgrado en Ciencias e Ingeniería de la Computación de la
 UNAM y actualmente me encuentro trabajando dentro del Visual Computing
 Group en Intel Guadalajara Dentro de dicho grupo tenemos la necesidad de
 contratar a un gerente para el área de gráficos y media es por esto le
 pido de la manera más atenta haga llegar esta oferta de trabajo a alumnos
 y egresados del posgrado quizá a alguno de ellos le gustaría aplicar para
 dicha plaza

 A continuación le envío la descripción de dicha oferta

 

 Graphics & Media Eng Manager  
 Description
  In this position your responsibilities will include but not be limited
 to

 Planning

  Participating in the team's planning process
 Team Contribution
  Working to improve group dynamics by drawing others out moderating
 conflict
  Keeping discussion on track and ensures group efforts are in line with
 mission
  Participating on crossfunctional divisional or corporate task forces

 Leadership

  Taking intelligent risks
  Striving for technical innovation and embraces change
  Suggesting creative solutions and sees ideas through to completion
  Known beyond our team as an expert in one of more areas typically one
 of the interfaces we are responsible for

 Mentoring

  Evaluating and providing feedback on the effectiveness and efficiency of
 other engineers validation choices
  Sharing personal experiences and learning's with other engineers to help
 them understand and solve similar problems
  Encouraging engineers to communicate difficulties and problems by
 demonstrating personal interest
  Creating assignments that provide a positive 'win' experience and the
 necessary technical background to move on to more complex tasks
  Working 'side by side' with other engineers as needed to help them learn
 a new skill or come up to speed quickly

 Ownership

  Viewing project from the manager's role  Activities indicate employee
 is worrying as much about the project as the manager
  Effectively helping management set direction
  Setting an example for all other team members andor is a positive
 influence on other team members

 Innovation

  Recognizing and driving productivity improvements at the team level
 Qualifications
  You should possess a Bachelor of Science degree with  years experience
 or a Master of Science degree with  years experience Additional
 qualifications include

  Demonstrates a strong ownership role in challenging technical
 assignments which require crossteam interaction
  Demonstrates a strong ownership role on an interface with significant
 technical challenges
  Ability to complete many tasks by directing the activities of others
  Ability to take ambiguous assignments and create relevant clear goals
 and plans to accomplish the assignment

 Technical Skills

  Solid math background and programming experience with D graphics APIs
 and experience with either DirectX or OpenGL
  Digital Imaging Processing
  Strong knowledge of Digital Imaging Processing
  Good understanding of Direct Video Acceleration  DXVA  and Vista
 Enhance Video Renderer EVR
  Understanding of video formats MPEG color space picture type and
 others

 Level of supervision

  Limited supervision
  Recognizes problems and identifies solutions independently raising to
 management only as required
  Capability of effectively driving crossteam task forces to debug
 difficult problems Frequently identifies productivity andor process
 improvements and creates or drives solutions

 Planning

  Ability to foresee problems and effectively uses mitigation andor
 contingency plans to address

 Team Contribution
  More often in a leadership or facilitative role
  Often a motivator to rest of team

 Leadership

  Seizes opportunities to contribute
  Ability to make tough decisions weighing options and tradeoffs
  Pushes back on issues with rationale and offers alternatives
  Willingness to stand up for higher idea and defend it

 Communication

  Communicates effectively with entire team including many others senior
 management


 Ownership

  Program success
  Highest level of results orientation
  Ability to make effective management level presentations

 

 De antemano muchas gracias

 
 Victor J Lopez
 Software Validation Engineer
 VCG ProV
 Intel GDC

 diagrams Diagrams  First Call for Papers
BODY 
Apologies if you receive this more than once



DDDDDDDDDDDDDDD
Diagrams 

Sixth International Conference on the
Theory and Application of Diagrams

httpwwwdiagramsconferenceorg
diagrams@diagramsconferenceorg

 August 
Portland Oregon USA



DDDDDDDDDDDDDDD

Diagrams is an international and interdisciplinary conference series
covering all aspects of research on the theory and application of
diagrams

Recent advances in technology have enabled the use of diagrams sketches
and other visualizations to become an integral part of our lives For
effective communication with these novel and sophisticated visual
representations we need insight into how diagrams are used how they
are represented which types are available and when it is appropriate to
use them These concerns have triggered a surge of interest in the study
of diagrammatic notations for communication cognition creative
thought computation and problemsolving

The study of diagrammatic notations and their use must be pursued as an
interdisciplinary endeavour Diagrams is the only conference series that
provides a united forum for all areas that are concerned with the study
of diagrams for example architecture artificial intelligence
cartography cognitive science computer science education graphic
design history of science humancomputer interaction linguistics
logic mathematics philosophy psychology and software modelling

Diagrams  is the sixth event in this conference series which was
launched in Edinburgh in  Diagrams attracts a large number of
researchers from virtually all related fields mentioned placing the
conference as a major international event in the area

Diagrams  will be colocated with the nd Annual Meeting of the
Cognitive Science Society Cogsci This colocation will provide a
lively and stimulating environment enabling researchers from related
communities to exchange ideas and more widely disseminate research
results

Diagrams  will consist of sessions including presentations of
refereed papers posters and also tutorial and workshop sessions For
the first time in history of Diagrams we will organize workshops and
postgraduate student sessions We invite submissions of

 long research papers  pages
 short research papers  pages
 posters  pages
 tutorial proposals  page; see the conference web page for full
details
 workshop proposals  page; see the conference web page for full
details

that focus on any aspect of diagrams research Long papers should
present original research results Short papers and posters should
present original research contributions position or problem statements
summarise software to support the use of diagrams or integrate results
published elsewhere which are of interest to the Diagrams community

All submissions will be fully peer reviewed The proceedings will be
published by Springer in their Lecture Notes in Computer Science series
wwwspringercomlncs

Full details on the preparation of submissions can be found on the
conference web site wwwdiagramsconferenceorg

Topics of interest include but are not limited to

 applications of diagrams
 computational models of reasoning with and interpretation of
diagrams
 design of diagrammatic notations
 diagram understanding by humans or machines
 diagram aesthetics and layout
 educational uses of diagrams
 graphical communication
 heterogeneous notations involving diagrams
 history of diagrammatic notations
 information visualization using diagrams
 novel uses of diagrams
 psychological issues pertaining to perception comprehension or
production of diagrams
 reasoning with diagrams
 software to support the use of diagrams
 theoretical aspects of diagrams including for example classification
and formalization
 usability issues concerning diagrams


Important dates
DDDDDDDDDDDDDDD

Notification for papers and tutorials  March 
Notification for posters  March

Diagrams  conference  August

Estimado a Colega

Los departamentos de Ingeniería Eléctrica Control Automático y 
Computación del CINVESTAVIPN invitan a la comunidad científica y a 
los profesionales de la ingeniería a participar en la

th International Conference on Electrical Engineering Computing 
Science and Automatic Control
CCE Formerly known as ICEEE

Los dias    y  de Noviembre de  en la Ciudad de Toluca en 
las instalaciones de la facultad de Ingeniería de la Universidad 
Autónoma del Estado de México

Esta congreso tiene como objetivo promover la vinculación entre los 
sectores productivo y académico del país ofreciendo a estudiantes 
investigadores y profesionistas un foro propicio para presentar e 
informarse de los avances y nuevos desarrollos realizados en Ingeniería 
Eléctrica Electrónica Computación Control Automático y áreas afines 
El evento comprende la presentación de ponencias libres así como de 
conferencias plenarias ofrecidas por invitados tanto nacionales como 
extranjeros de reconocido prestigio Así mismo los días  y  de 
Noviembre se ofrecerán varios cursos como preámbulo de este importante 
evento Para mayor información por favor visite nuestra página 
httpccecinvestavmx

Se aceptarán ponencias originales en cualquiera de las siguientes áreas 
Ciencias de la Computación Ingeniería en Computación Comunicaciones 
Control Automático Bioelectrónica Biomedicina Mecatrónica 
Electrónica del Estados Sólido Semiconductores Sensores y Actuadotes 
Sistemas de Potencia

Los trabajos serán evaluados por un Comité Técnico formado por expertos 
nacionales e internacionales y aquellos aceptados para su presentación 
serán publicados en las memorias CCE  con el patrocinio de Electron 
Devices Society EDS del Institute of Electrical and Electronics 
Engineering IEEE Dichas memorias serán entregadas en el evento

Los autores de los mejores trabajos presentados en el congreso serán 
contactados posteriormente para participar en la publicación de un libro 
con versiones sustancialmente extendidas de los mismos

Fecha límite para entrega de artículos  de Julio de 
Notificación de aceptaciónrechazo  de Agosto de 
Entrega de artículos en formato definitivo  de Septiembre de 


Sin otro particular por el momento quedamos de Usted

Atentamente

 Position Tenure track professorship in Computer Sciences

 Required qualifications PhD in Computer Sciences HCI Software 
 engineering Cooperative technologies Interaction design and a 
 strong record of research and scholarship c  years of experience 

 desirable in this domain Habilitation for French and German 
 candidates

 Contract work The successful candidate will be offered a first 
 contract for a duration of three years At the issue of this period 

  to the agreement of the Board of Administration of the 
 University HeShe could be offered a permanent position

 Salary according to experience  to  Euros per month

 Activities
 The candidate will participate in teaching activities in the 
 Information Systems Engineer cursus and Master programmes 
 Information Technologies for Knowledge and Networks Management
 In particular the candidate will be in charge of teaching Rapid 
 prototyping design collaborative technologies and interaction design
 The successful applicant will contribute to the development of the 
 TechCICO laboratory which is part of the Charles Delaunay Institute 

 FRE CNRS 
 HeShe will conduct research in specialized areas of computer 
 science Human Computer Interaction and cooperative technologies
 Main research activities
  Establish a comprehensive research program in the area of HCI and 

 cooperative technologies;
  Explore for grant opportunities national and European
  Establish collaboration with industrial partners
  Tutor PhD and MSc students
  Participate in the activities of national and European research 
 networks
 The candidat will also participate to the scientific animation of a 

 HCICooperative technologies group and will have an active 
 participation in national and international research networks

 vitae and cover letter to

 CFP st Mexican Workshop on Pattern Recognition MWPR
BODY 
Dear Luis A Pineda Corts

 PLEASE CIRCULATE this CFP among your colleagues and students

 MWPRnd CFP

MEXICAN WORKSHOP ON PATTERN RECOGNITION MWPR
November   Guadalajara
URL httpcccinaoepmx~mwpr

 GENERAL INFORMATION 

The st Mexican Workshop on Pattern Recognition MWPR will be held in 
Guadalajara Mexico MWPR is organized by CINVESTAV Unidad 
Guadalajara Mxico and the Mexican Association for Computer Vision Neural 
Computing and Robotics MACVNR MWRP is sponsored by the Computer 
Science Department of the National Institute of Astrophysics Optics and 
Electronics INAOE and the Center for Computing Research of the National 
Polytechnic Institute CICIPN
MWPR will be a forum for exchanging scientific results and 
experiences as well as sharing new knowledge and increasing the 
cooperation between research groups in pattern recognition and related 
areas in Mexico

 CHAIRS 

Dr Jose Francisco Martinez Trinidad INAOE Puebla Mxico
Dr Jesus Ariel Carrasco Ochoa INAOE Puebla Mxico
Dr Eduardo Bayro Corrochano CINVESTAVGDL Mexico 
Dr Humberto Sossa Azuela CICIPN Mexico
Dr Jorge Rivera Rovelo Universidad Anhuac Mayab Merida Mexico
Dr Jaime Silverio Ortegn Aguilar Universidad de Quintana Roo   

 TOPICS 

Authors are invited to submit contributions includes but not limited to 
the following topics

Computer Vision 
Data Mining 
Natural Language Processing and Recognition 
Discrete Geometry 
Document Processing and Recognition 
Fuzzy and Hybrid Techniques in Pattern Recognition 
Image Coding Processing and Analysis 
Industrial and Medical Applications of Pattern Recognition 
Logical Combinatorial Pattern Recognition 
Mathematical Morphology 
Neural Networks 
Artificial Intelligent Techniques and Recognition 
Pattern Recognition Principles 
Robotics & Remote Sensing Applications of Pattern Recognition 
Shape and Texture Analysis 
Signal Processing and Analysis 
Special Hardware Architectures 
Statistical & Structural Pattern Recognition 
Voice and Speech Recognition 
Parallel and Distributed Pattern Recognition 


 PAPER SUBMISSION 

All the  Apages papers must be submitted in English but could be 
presented at the conference in Spanish or English All submissions will be 
peer reviewed by the Scientific Committee for originality technical 
content and relevance The final acceptance will be based upon double 
blind peer review of the fulllength paper
All accepted papers will be published in Proceedings of the Conference in 
the Journal Research in Computing Science ISSN ISSN   Indexed by 
Latndex
The papers should be submitted electronically before August   The 
papers should be prepared following the instructions from Springer LNCS 
series see httpwwwspringerdecomplncsinstructtypeinstpdf 
Submission implies the willingness of at least one of the authors to 
register and to present the communication at the conference if it is 
accepted 

 JOURNAL SPECIAL ISSUES 

A selection of the best papers will be invited to submit an extended 
version to Computacin y Sistemas ISSN  Indexed by CONACyT 
Ejournal Latndex Peridica SciELO and Redalyc


 IMPORTANT DATES 

Submission of papers August  
Notification of acceptance September  
Cameraready September  

 CONTACT 

Organizing Committee
mwpr@cccinaoepmx
<httpcccinaoepmx~mwpr
More information about MWPR will be available soon Watch this space

 International Conference CCE Invitation
BODY  Abril de  

Los Departamentos de Ingeniería Eléctrica Control automático y
Computación del CINVESTAVIPN invitan a la comunidad científica y a los
profesionales de la Ingeniería a participar en la

th International Conference on Electrical Engineering Computing Science
and Automatic Control CCE
Formerly known as ICEEE

los días     de Noviembre de  en la Ciudad de Toluca en
las instalaciones de la Facultad de Ingeniería de la Universidad Autónoma
del Estado de México

Este congreso tiene como objetivo promover la vinculación entre los
sectores productivo y académico del país ofreciendo a estudiantes
investigadores y profesionistas un foro propicio para presentar e
informarse de los avances y nuevos desarrollos realizados en Ingeniería
Eléctrica Electrónica Computación Control Automático y áreas afines El
evento comprende la presentación de ponencias libres así como de
conferencias plenarias ofrecidas por invitados tanto nacionales como
extranjeros de reconocido prestigio Asimismo los días  y  de
Noviembre se ofrecerán varios cursos como preámbulo de este importante
evento Para mayor información por favor visite nuestra página
httpccecinvestavmx

Se aceptarán ponencias originales en cualquiera de las siguientes áreas
Ciencias de la Computación Ingeniería en Computación Comunicaciones
Control Automático Bioelectrónica Biomedicina Mecatrónica Electrónica
del Estado Sólido Semiconductores Sensores y Actuadores Sistemas de
Potencia

Los trabajos serán evaluados por un Comité Técnico formado por expertos
nacionales e internacionales y aquellos aceptados para su presentación
serán publicados en las memorias CCE  con el patrocinio de Electron
Devices Society EDS del Institute of Electrical and Electronics
Engineers IEEE Dichas memorias serán entregadas en el evento

Los autores de los mejores trabajos presentados en el congreso serán
contactados posteriormente para participar en la publicación de un libro
con versiones sustancialmente extendidas de los mismos


Fecha límite para entrega de artículos 			 de Julio de 
Notificación de aceptaciónrechazo				 de Agosto de 
Entrega de artículos en formato definitivo			 de Septiembre de 



Atentamente


Dr José Antonio Moreno Cadenas Dr Carlos A Coello Coello Dr
Alexander Poznyak Gorbatch
Presidentes del Comité Organizador
CCE 


April    

Dear Professor Student and Professional

On behalf of the Organizing Committee of the th International Conference
on Electrical Engineering Computing Science and Automatic Control CCE
Formerly known as ICEEE we are pleased to invite you to participate in
this event by submitting original technical articles

This event is sponsored by the Electron Device Society EDS of the
Institute of Electrical and Electronics Engineers IEEE in which the
Conference Proceedings edition has registered both ISBN and IEEE Catalog
numbers

Location Toluca Mexico at premises of Facultad de Ingeniería of the
Universidad Autónoma del Estado de México

Conference November   

Important Dates

Submission of manuscripts 				July  
Notification of acceptancerejection 		August  
Final revised manuscripts 				September  

The complete information of this academic and scientific conference can be
found at the conferences site

httpccecinvestavmx

The authors of the best papers presented at the conference will be
contacted after the event for submitting extended versions of their works
for possible inclusion in a book to be published in English

We would highly appreciate it if you could resend this invitation to any
of your colleagues who might be interested in this event

Sincerely


Dr José Antonio Moreno Cadenas
Dr Carlos Coello Coello
Dr Alexander Poznyak Gorbatch

content and relevance The final acceptance will be based upon double 
blind peer review of the fulllength paper
All accepted papers will be published in Proceedings of the Conference in 
the Journal Research in Computing Science ISSN ISSN   Indexed by 
Latndex
The papers should be submitted electronically before August   The 
papers should be prepared following the instructions from Springer LNCS 
series see httpwwwspringerdecomplncsinstructtypeinstpdf 
Submission implies the willingness of at least one of the authors to 
register and to present the communication at the conference if it is 
accepted 

 JOURNAL SPECIAL ISSUES 

A selection of the best papers will be invited to submit an extended 
version to Computacin y Sistemas ISSN  Indexed by CONACyT 
Ejournal Latndex Peridica SciELO and Redalyc


 IMPORTANT DATES 

Submission of papers August  
Notification of acceptance September  
Cameraready September

mwpr@cccinaoepmx
<httpcccinaoepmx~mwpr
More information about MWPR will be available soon Watch this space
